<TagTitle slot="title">

# Client Answers Endpoints

</TagTitle>

</Tag>

<Operation>

<OperationTitleSection slot="title">

## <Pill variant="primary"><b>POST</b></Pill> /rest/api/v1/createanswer \{#operation-createanswer\}

</OperationTitleSection>

<OperationSummarySection slot="summary">

_Create Answer_

</OperationSummarySection>

<OperationDescriptionSection slot="description">

Create a user-generated Answer that contains a question and answer.

</OperationDescriptionSection>

<OperationCodeSamplesSection slot="code-samples">

>

                   name: &quot;user&quot;,&NewLine;                  },&NewLine;                },&NewLine;              ],&NewLine;            },&NewLine;          },&NewLine;          role: &quot;EDITOR&quot;,&NewLine;        },&NewLine;        {&NewLine;          person: {&NewLine;            name: &quot;George Clooney&quot;,&NewLine;            obfuscatedId: &quot;abc123&quot;,&NewLine;            metadata: {&NewLine;              type: &quot;FULL_TIME&quot;,&NewLine;              title: &quot;Actor&quot;,&NewLine;              department: &quot;Movies&quot;,&NewLine;              email: &quot;george@example.com&quot;,&NewLine;              location: &quot;Hollywood, CA&quot;,&NewLine;              phone: &quot;6505551234&quot;,&NewLine;              photoUrl: &quot;https://example.com/george.jpg&quot;,&NewLine;              startDate: new RFCDate(&quot;2000-01-23&quot;),&NewLine;              datasourceProfile: [&NewLine;                {&NewLine;                  datasource: &quot;github&quot;,&NewLine;                  handle: &quot;&lt;value&gt;&quot;,&NewLine;                },&NewLine;                {&NewLine;                  datasource: &quot;github&quot;,&NewLine;                  handle: &quot;&lt;value&gt;&quot;,&NewLine;                },&NewLine;                {&NewLine;                  datasource: &quot;github&quot;,&NewLine;                  handle: &quot;&lt;value&gt;&quot;,&NewLine;                },&NewLine;              ],&NewLine;              querySuggestions: {&NewLine;                suggestions: [&NewLine;                  {&NewLine;                    query: &quot;app:github type:pull author:mortimer&quot;,&NewLine;                    label: &quot;Mortimer's PRs&quot;,&NewLine;                    datasource: &quot;github&quot;,&NewLine;                  },&NewLine;                ],&NewLine;              },&NewLine;              inviteInfo: {&NewLine;                invites: [&NewLine;                  {},&NewLine;                  {},&NewLine;                ],&NewLine;              },&NewLine;              badges: [&NewLine;                {&NewLine;                  key: &quot;deployment_name_new_hire&quot;,&NewLine;                  displayName: &quot;New hire&quot;,&NewLine;      },&NewLine;    },&NewLine;  });&NewLine;&NewLine;  console.log(result);&NewLine;}&NewLine;&NewLine;run();&NewLine;"

##### audienceFilters \{#operation-createanswer+responses+200+application-json+audiencefilters\}

A list of filters for the query. An AND is assumed between different facetFilters. For example, owner Sumeet and type Spreadsheet shows documents that are by Sumeet AND are Spreadsheets.

<ExpandablePropertyTitle slot="title">

##### groupName \{#operation-createanswer+responses+200+application-json+audiencefilters+facetfilter+groupname\}

</ExpandablePropertyTitle>

<ExpandablePropertyDescription slot="description">

Indicates the value of a facet, if any, that the given facet is grouped under. This is only used for nested facets, for example, fieldName could be owner and groupName would be Spreadsheet if showing all owners for spreadsheets as a nested facet.

</ExpandablePropertyDescription>

<ExpandablePropertyExamples slot="examples">

_Example:_

```
Spreadsheet
```

</ExpandablePropertyExamples>

</ExpandableProperty>

</ExpandablePropertyTitle>

<ExpandablePropertyDescription slot="description">

Within a single FacetFilter, the values are to be treated like an OR. For example, fieldName type with values [EQUALS Presentation, EQUALS Spreadsheet] means we want to show a document if it's a Presentation OR a Spreadsheet.

</ExpandablePropertyDescription>

<ExpandablePropertyBreakouts slot="breakouts">

<Embed slot="embed">

<EmbedTrigger slot="trigger" embedTitle="values" triggerText="View values details">

<Embedvalues />

</EmbedTrigger>

</Embed>

</ExpandablePropertyBreakouts>

</ExpandableProperty>

</ExpandableBreakoutProperties>

</ExpandableBreakout>

</ExpandablePropertyBreakouts>

</ExpandableProperty>

<OperationTitleSection slot="title">

## <Pill variant="primary"><b>POST</b></Pill> /rest/api/v1/deleteanswer \{#operation-deleteanswer\}

</OperationTitleSection>

<OperationSummarySection slot="summary">

_Delete Answer_

</OperationSummarySection>

<OperationDescriptionSection slot="description">

Delete an existing user-generated Answer.

</OperationDescriptionSection>

<OperationCodeSamplesSection slot="code-samples">

  dependencyUrlPrefix="/glean-try-it-now"
  packageName="@gleanwork/api-client"

```curl
curl https://{instance}-be.glean.com/rest/api/v1/deleteanswer \
 -X POST \
 -H 'Authorization: Bearer YOUR_APITOKEN_HERE' \
 -d '{
  "id": "3"
}'
```

  hasDescription
  hasExamples
>

<ExpandablePropertyTitle slot="title">

##### docId \{#operation-deleteanswer+request+docid\}

</ExpandablePropertyTitle>

<ExpandablePropertyDescription slot="description">

Glean Document ID of the Answer. The Glean Document ID is supported for cases where the Answer ID isn't available. If both are available, using the Answer ID is preferred.

</ExpandablePropertyDescription>

<ExpandablePropertyExamples slot="examples">

_Example:_

```
ANSWERS_answer_3
```

</ExpandablePropertyExamples>

</ExpandableProperty>

  id="operation-deleteanswer+request+id"

  typeAnnotations={`[{"title":"required","variant":"warning"}]`}
  expandByDefault
  hasDescription
  hasExamples
>

<ExpandablePropertyTitle slot="title">

##### id \{#operation-deleteanswer+request+id\}

</ExpandablePropertyTitle>

<ExpandablePropertyDescription slot="description">

The opaque ID of the Answer.

</ExpandablePropertyDescription>

<ExpandablePropertyExamples slot="examples">

_Example:_

```
3
```

</ExpandablePropertyExamples>

<SectionContent slot="content" id="operation-editanswer+code-samples+curl">

<CodeSample>

```curl
curl https://{instance}-be.glean.com/rest/api/v1/editanswer \
 -X POST \
 -H 'Authorization: Bearer YOUR_APITOKEN_HERE' \
 -d '{
  "id": "3"
}'
```

<ExpandablePropertyTitle slot="title">

##### audienceFilters \{#operation-editanswer+request+audiencefilters\}

</ExpandablePropertyTitle>

<ExpandablePropertyDescription slot="description">

A list of filters for the query. An AND is assumed between different facetFilters. For example, owner Sumeet and type Spreadsheet shows documents that are by Sumeet AND are Spreadsheets.

</ExpandablePropertyDescription>

<ExpandablePropertyBreakouts slot="breakouts">

<ExpandableBreakoutProperties slot="properties">

>

<ExpandableProperty
  id="operation-editanswer+request+audiencefilters+facetfilter+groupname"
  entryId="audienceFilters_FacetFilter_groupName"
  parentId="audienceFilters_FacetFilter"
  typeInfo={`{"label":"string","linkedLabel":"string","children":[],"breakoutSubTypes":{}}`}
  typeAnnotations={`[]`}
  hasDescription
  hasExamples
>

<ExpandablePropertyTitle slot="title">

##### groupName \{#operation-editanswer+request+audiencefilters+facetfilter+groupname\}

</ExpandablePropertyTitle>

<ExpandablePropertyDescription slot="description">

Indicates the value of a facet, if any, that the given facet is grouped under. This is only used for nested facets, for example, fieldName could be owner and groupName would be Spreadsheet if showing all owners for spreadsheets as a nested facet.

</ExpandablePropertyDescription>

<ExpandablePropertyExamples slot="examples">

_Example:_

```
Spreadsheet
```

</ExpandablePropertyExamples>

</ExpandableProperty>

<ExpandableProperty
  id="operation-editanswer+request+audiencefilters+facetfilter+values"
  entryId="audienceFilters_FacetFilter_values"
  parentId="audienceFilters_FacetFilter"
  typeInfo={`{"label":"array","linkedLabel":"<a href=\\"#operation-editanswer+request+audiencefilters+facetfilter+values+facetfiltervalue\\">FacetFilterValue</a>","children":[{"label":"FacetFilterValue","linkedLabel":"<a href=\\"#operation-editanswer+request+audiencefilters+facetfilter+values+facetfiltervalue\\">FacetFilterValue</a>","children":[],"breakoutSubTypes":{}}],"breakoutSubTypes":{}}`}
  typeAnnotations={`[]`}
  hasDescription
  hasEmbed
>

<ExpandablePropertyTitle slot="title">

##### values \{#operation-editanswer+request+audiencefilters+facetfilter+values\}

</ExpandablePropertyTitle>

<ExpandablePropertyDescription slot="description">

Within a single FacetFilter, the values are to be treated like an OR. For example, fieldName type with values [EQUALS Presentation, EQUALS Spreadsheet] means we want to show a document if it's a Presentation OR a Spreadsheet.

</ExpandablePropertyDescription>

<ExpandablePropertyBreakouts slot="breakouts">

</EmbedTrigger>

</Embed>

</ExpandablePropertyBreakouts>

</ExpandableProperty>

</ExpandableBreakoutProperties>

</ExpandableBreakout>

</ExpandablePropertyBreakouts>

</ExpandableProperty>

  hasDescription

<ExpandablePropertyTitle slot="title">

##### boardId \{#operation-editanswer+request+boardid\}

</ExpandablePropertyTitle>

<ExpandablePropertyDescription slot="description">

The parent board ID of this Answer, or 0 if it's a floating Answer. Adding Answers to Answer Boards is no longer permitted.

</ExpandablePropertyDescription>

</ExpandableProperty>

<ExpandablePropertyTitle slot="title">

##### audienceFilters \{#operation-editanswer+responses+200+application-json+audiencefilters\}

</ExpandablePropertyTitle>

<ExpandablePropertyDescription slot="description">

A list of filters for the query. An AND is assumed between different facetFilters. For example, owner Sumeet and type Spreadsheet shows documents that are by Sumeet AND are Spreadsheets.

</ExpandablePropertyDescription>

<ExpandablePropertyBreakouts slot="breakouts">

<ExpandableBreakout
  id="operation-editanswer+responses+200+application-json+audiencefilters+facetfilter"

<ExpandablePropertyTitle slot="title">

##### fieldName \{#operation-editanswer+responses+200+application-json+audiencefilters+facetfilter+fieldname\}

</ExpandablePropertyTitle>

<ExpandablePropertyExamples slot="examples">

_Example:_

```
owner
```

</ExpandablePropertyExamples>

</ExpandableProperty>

<ExpandableProperty
  id="operation-editanswer+responses+200+application-json+audiencefilters+facetfilter+groupname"
  entryId="audienceFilters_FacetFilter_groupName"
  parentId="audienceFilters_FacetFilter"
  typeInfo={`{"label":"string","linkedLabel":"string","children":[],"breakoutSubTypes":{}}`}
  typeAnnotations={`[]`}
  hasDescription
  hasExamples
>

<ExpandablePropertyTitle slot="title">

##### groupName \{#operation-editanswer+responses+200+application-json+audiencefilters+facetfilter+groupname\}

</ExpandablePropertyTitle>

<ExpandablePropertyDescription slot="description">

Indicates the value of a facet, if any, that the given facet is grouped under. This is only used for nested facets, for example, fieldName could be owner and groupName would be Spreadsheet if showing all owners for spreadsheets as a nested facet.

</ExpandablePropertyDescription>

<ExpandablePropertyExamples slot="examples">

_Example:_

```
Spreadsheet
```

</ExpandablePropertyExamples>

</ExpandableProperty>

<ExpandableProperty
  id="operation-editanswer+responses+200+application-json+audiencefilters+facetfilter+values"
  entryId="audienceFilters_FacetFilter_values"
  parentId="audienceFilters_FacetFilter"
  typeInfo={`{"label":"array","linkedLabel":"<a href=\\"#operation-editanswer+responses+200+application-json+audiencefilters+facetfilter+values+facetfiltervalue\\">FacetFilterValue</a>","children":[{"label":"FacetFilterValue","linkedLabel":"<a href=\\"#operation-editanswer+responses+200+application-json+audiencefilters+facetfilter+values+facetfiltervalue\\">FacetFilterValue</a>","children":[],"breakoutSubTypes":{}}],"breakoutSubTypes":{}}`}
  typeAnnotations={`[]`}
  hasDescription
  hasEmbed
>

<ExpandablePropertyTitle slot="title">

##### values \{#operation-editanswer+responses+200+application-json+audiencefilters+facetfilter+values\}

</ExpandablePropertyTitle>

<ExpandablePropertyDescription slot="description">

Within a single FacetFilter, the values are to be treated like an OR. For example, fieldName type with values [EQUALS Presentation, EQUALS Spreadsheet] means we want to show a document if it's a Presentation OR a Spreadsheet.

</ExpandablePropertyDescription>

</EmbedTrigger>

</Embed>

</ExpandablePropertyBreakouts>

</ExpandableProperty>

</ExpandableBreakoutProperties>

</ExpandableBreakout>

</ExpandablePropertyBreakouts>

</ExpandableProperty>

</ExpandablePropertyTitle>

<ExpandablePropertyDescription slot="description">

A list of filters for the query. An AND is assumed between different facetFilters. For example, owner Sumeet and type Spreadsheet shows documents that are by Sumeet AND are Spreadsheets.

</ExpandablePropertyDescription>
